<Rating>5</Rating><Text>I walked into the Temple in ignorace; I left the Temple enlightened.

Was fortunate enough to see this beautiful temple. Walk in and ascended the marble stairs (no leather, no shoes). I was confronted by a beautiful statue of the first Tirthankier (appologize for spelling). Realising that I was an outsider a woman who spoke beautifully and reverently walked me around the entire temple and basically gave me a private in-depth tour of this religion of peace. Nothing asked in return. One of their primary tenants I found was charity. "Why raise your standard of living when you can raise your standard of giving?"

I finished my tour and was permitted to ask questions (but not of those doing Pooja {quite please}) and meditate on the temple floor. Charity boxes are located for your donations. I recommend a donation; the temple itself is a Museum to the culture.< /Text>< pictures>

Best Mexican fast food restaurant I have visited in Sandiego.  I am always worried about stopping at a fast food Mexican restaurant.  Most of the time the quality of the food is not there.  However, the food is very good here.  The other day I went to Sonic and I spent $16.  At Castanedas, I paid $10, and the food quality was better.  Everything tasted fresh and made to the order.

4 stars for atmosphere (for goodness sake, it is a fast food restaurant)</review>

< Date>

<Rate>4</Rate>< text>
I am in love with the Carne Asada Fries from Castanedas.  My favorite thing about them is the fresh cut fries which so many people complain about.  Maybe it's just me, but I prefer a fresh cut potato to a bagged frozen french fry.  Sure, they may be soggier than the frozen, but I'd gladly take a soggy fresh fry over a crisp frozen one any day.  I think the meat is very good and of the many times I have visited never had any gristle or fat on my carne asada. There is plenty of cheese and sour cream.  The only bummer to me is the guacamole.  It's the reason for the 4 stars instead of 5.  Unfortunately this guacamole tastes watered down and doesn't taste much like avocado.  I wish they would not water it down.

The service has always been great.  I have not had any issues with my orders whether ordering inside or through the drive thru.  The staff is always friendly and pleasant.  It's one of my top choice to order carne asada fries.</text>

<Text>The main reason I'm giving this place one star is because the customer service was TERRIBLE. For more details, read on...

The first time I went to this restaurant, about a week ago, I ordered the rolled tacos and was extremely satisfied. The rolled tacos were perfect and the hot sauce was soooo yummy! I literally wanted to drink it. I thought, "I have to try some other dishes at this place."

The second time, I decided to try a burrito. I'm a pretty picky eater, so I usually order the plain carne asada burrito. I know that this can be difficult to understand (especially through the drive-thru) so I usually try to speak and enunciate clearly and I also give the instructions twice. I asked for a Plain Carne Asada Burrito, with the meat only, please.

I get up to the window and my total is $8.46. Expensive but I thought it might be worth it.

I drive all the way back to work, park, take a bite and immediately notice it is not plain.

I drive back to this place, tell them that I asked very clearly and specifically for a plain carne asada burrito. I was expecting to get some kind-of discounted price, a free drink, chips and salsa, a side of beans, ANYTHING to make up for your poor customer service. Nothing. Just a "sorry." I would have even been happy with a more sincere apology. I probably would have come back in the future if the situation was somehow reconciled.

Instead, you have lost a customer and you get this enlightening review!

Side note: The hot sauce somehow changed flavors completely in a week and the burrito honestly tasted better without it.</Text>< username>
Lacey Houshar< /username>

<review>I went into this store on a long shot, not really expecting to find what I was looking for. Within minutes I was able to locate exactly what I had hoped to find so that when the clerk offers his assistance, I kindly decline.So pleased I was in this moment that I venture to take a look around and I notice the key making station. The same clerk was there, along with the cashier and some other dude. I ask the clerk for his help in removing three keys to be copied. I tell him I need a total of five keys and he repeats back my request, just to confirm and then proceeds to hand the keys over to another guy. I figure that I don't need to wait and continue to look around, I find out later that I couldn't have been more wrong!
Having picked up a few other items I go to check out, the clerk tells me my keys are all in the bag. It wasn't until I go out to my car when I find only two of my original keys had been copied. My pad lock key was just gone altogether. I go back in and tell the cashier and she insists they were in the bag. With key guy, standing right there I ask about my other key. He just stares at me with not one glimmer of recognition. I turn to the clerk, who was my only hope and think surely he must remember me or my key.  I am shocked when he simply states, "there were 10". Ten?? He is useless, Deep breath, I am feeling  a darkness enter the store as I stand there while the guy who made the key and this ugly cashier both just look at me  and tell me there was nothing they can do and they meant that, literally. The clerk, the key maker, the cashier did NOTHING to acknowledge my concerns let alone actually finding my key! They did however, completely dismiss me, and that was when I thought, these people are trying to make me look absolutely crazy! I go back to my car, no key, I go back in with determination but honestly not knowing how bad this situation was going to get. I make a plea, once again to the cashier but her nature is just rude and perhaps evil. I count to ten, take another deep breathe...I feel  eerily calm and I just know I'm about to lose it. I so don't want to go there, the countdown begins but thank Jesus for divine interventions! Suddenly,  I hear someone say, "Is this your Brinks key"? I look up by the key making machine to see this older woman, a clerk that I hadn't seen before. I swear she just came out of nowhere. I say "yes, yes it is. Thank you so very much". I leave thanking God to be out of that weird, wicked place and even happier to escape the potential horror show of losing ones temper.
I honestly don't know what was going on with these people. What they did was so shockingly unnatural and so random, a most frightening the experience, indeed. Buyer Beware!< /review><Pictures>None</Pictures><response>None</response>< Gmap_id>

My reservation was last minute and I was VERY stressed, as I had to move my entire home into a storage unit because the new house wasn't going to be ready in time. The customer service people on the phone couldn't have been nicer or more helpful in figuring out what I needed, and making sure I got the Internet promotional rate. I was happy with that process (and it was nice for something to go right for a change, because up to this point, EVERYTHING that could go wrong with my move had gone wrong - TERRIBLY WRONG - EXCEPT for my storage unit rental experience. The phone reservation went well and I got a good deal, so I was happy. THEN, when I showed up to the facility to pay & get my unit, the Property Manager, Katie went above and beyond to help me through the process...TWO TIMES!...I had to rent a second, smaller unit later that day because I have WAY TOO MUCH STUFF! She was pleasant, helpful, and didn't get frustrated with me and my 1000 questions. I highly recommend this place...particularly the StorQuest on Frontage Rd. <user_name>Robert H< /user_name><Rate>5</Rate>< Review>
I've always wanted to try Ube Pancakes (a stack of purple pancakes with a ton of purple sauce), but from pictures, I felt that it would be way too sweet for my palate. That said, it was a great excuse to finally try them, as well as sample some of the other breakfast items that they offer.

With everything going on, they do offer to bring your order out to your car. If you call them a few minutes before you arrive, they make sure that they get your order to you promptly. The staff is very friendly over the phone, and are even more friendly when you see them in person.

As for those bright-looking purple pancakes? No hype at all! They are delicious! Very light and airy, and the sauce packs a nice authentic ube flavor that doesn't taste artificial. I've also tried their Chicken Tocino & Garlic Rice w/egg, and their Crispy Pork Sisig. Their flavors are unique and their carb to protein ratios are very balanced and generous. That said, you have no excuse but to stop by and give them a go!</Review>

<Review>Ube pancakes, not-oversweetened chai, everything is so delicious here!

I stopped by today to grab some lunch. After checking out their menu items on their website, I called in to place a to-go order and ordered the ube pancakes and a 20 oz. hot chai. Wait time was about 15 minutes, but that was fine because I was walking there. After arriving, I was pleasantly greeted by a staff member there and given my order once I paid for it. If you place a to-go drink order over the phone, they do put saran wrap over the lid after they make it if you aren't there to get it yet. A+ for cleanliness!

The ube pancakes were delicious. Easily, these were the best pancakes I've ever eaten. They're made of an ube batter, and you pour the ube sauce and toasted coconut flakes over them. Unlike traditional American pancakes, these are not overly sweet, which was perfect for me. The flavors of the ube and the texture of the pancakes made for a delicious meal!

The hot chai was great as well. This was most likely the best chai I've ever drank in the Bay Area. At Hub's, you're actually able to taste the flavors of the chai rather than tasting sips of sweetener (*cough cough* Starbucks).

Overall, 10/10 would recommend this small business if you're looking for breakfast, brunch, or breakfast-for-dinner! You definitely won't regret it!< /Review>< pics>
None< /pics>

Ube pancakes, not-oversweetened chai, everything is so delicious here!

I stopped by today to grab some lunch. After checking out their menu items on their website, I called in to place a to-go order and ordered the ube pancakes and a 20 oz. hot chai. Wait time was about 15 minutes, but that was fine because I was walking there. After arriving, I was pleasantly greeted by a staff member there and given my order once I paid for it. If you place a to-go drink order over the phone, they do put saran wrap over the lid after they make it if you aren't there to get it yet. A+ for cleanliness!

The ube pancakes were delicious. Easily, these were the best pancakes I've ever eaten. They're made of an ube batter, and you pour the ube sauce and toasted coconut flakes over them. Unlike traditional American pancakes, these are not overly sweet, which was perfect for me. The flavors of the ube and the texture of the pancakes made for a delicious meal!

The hot chai was great as well. This was most likely the best chai I've ever drank in the Bay Area. At Hub's, you're actually able to taste the flavors of the chai rather than tasting sips of sweetener (*cough cough* Starbucks).

Overall, 10/10 would recommend this small business if you're looking for breakfast, brunch, or breakfast-for-dinner! You definitely won't regret it!< /review>

<Review>One of the better bowling experiences. The place is a former AMF (the shoes, bowling balls, and other things still have AMF logos printed on them) but is still a unique enough experience.

Staff and service: Some are friendly and helpful, some aren't. So very hit or miss.

Food: Actually pretty good, for a bowling alley. Drinks are made well. We rented multiple lanes and we got unlimited drinks while we bowled. Loved the idea and it worked well!

Bowling: One of the best bowling experiences. The bowling balls are newer and better quality than most. Lanes are clean and maintained. Worth it to bowl here.</Review><Rating>4<//Rating>< pics>

< Review>
Absolutely fantastic bowling alley. A bit pricey if you're a novice bowler and want to get better, but there are constant new deals available to practice, and if you're a casual bowler with a party group, this is your place to be. Drinks are your average LA prices but seem to kick a little harder than normal. My friends and I consistently get what we call the fish bowl and share it.

Good music, good atmosphere, very clean and great staff.<//Review>

< Review>
The good: The lanes are relatively new and seem to be well kept. Overall, they have decent quality. They have service straight to the lanes for food which not all bowling alleys do these days.

The bad: It gets very expensive very quickly. Drinks, games, and food are all overpriced in my opinion.

The pro shop left the location and they no longer have one.

As for the bowling lanes themselves, they seemed to be pretty over oiled every time I went.

Overall: Not the best but not the worst either. If you don't mind going to a bit older style bowling alleys, there are much cheaper alternatives nearby with friendlier workers.< /Review>
